With this question, when we reached Lamhi's gate, on the 125th birth anniversary of Premchand ji, Mulayam Sarkar, who had taken his characters out of the book's form and embodied it at Lamhi's door, included Hori, old Kaki, Hamid, Halku, Ghisu, Madhav, Heera Moti have been seen staring at the neglect of Munshi Premchand sitting at Lamhi's gate ever since
 yah niraashaa unke us makaan main bhi dikhaai padi, jahaan yah paatr na sirf paidaa hue the balki jawan bhi hue the

 The Idgah where Premchand envisaged a society embracing in one color and one color without discrimination is today divided into castes and sub-castes due to personal selfishness and petty political will
 lihaaja aise samaaj main aaj ghisu or madhav kahin zyada marmaantak vednaa sah rahe hai

 Even in such times, with the help of "hamid" tongues to fight the lion, the question is still standing in front of the society that why these characters have become only entertainment for us today? Why Premchand's characters become proverbs for us? Why don't we have any means to ease their pain? Where will we take such a society? When progressive writers say that Premchand is relevant to us even today, then there is sadness in the mind because if Premchand is relevant today then surely there is somewhere in the society Hori, Budhi Kaki, Hamid, Halku, Ghisu, Madhav, Heera Pearls are alive

 chini taiyaar em-30 or es-30 kii keemat pichley saptahanth ke band str 3,850-4,000 rupee or 3,840-3,990 rupee se 100-100 rupee kii giravat ke saath 3,750-3,900 rupee or 3,740-3,890 rupee prati quintal par band hui
 Similarly, sugar mill delivery M-30 and S-30 closed at Rs 3,430-3,630 and Rs 3,420-3,620 per quintal over the weekend, showing a fall of Rs 40-40
